47 am It was placed in orbit approximately 19 minutes after launch

 uttar pradesh main "beti bachaao beti padhaao" abhiyaan kaa asar dikhaai dene laga he
 There has been an increase in 5 daughters per thousand sons in the entire state, although this figure still remains worrying
 uttar pradesh main 2016-17 main prati hajaar beton par 906 betiyaan janm leti thim, jo is saal 2017-18 main badhkar 911 ho gai he
 This has been revealed in the survey of maternal health and child planning of the government
 kahin dikhaa "beti bachaao beti padhaao" kaa asar to kahin beasarapradhanmantri modi kii muhimbeti bachaao beti padhaoka asar upi main kahin acha dikh rahaa he to kahin ab bhi beasar he
 In Lucknow, there has been an improvement in the average of the birth rates of sons and daughters, and the situation in Kanpur, Aligarh and Muzaffarnagar has worsened
 lakhanu main is saal prati hajaar 11 betiyon ke janm dar main badhotaree hui he
 There were 892 daughters per thousand sons in 2016-17, which has increased to 903 this year
 sirf lakhanu hi nahin puure pradesh main prati hajaar 5 betiyaan badi hai, jo achchhebhavishya kii ummidajagati he
 Apart from Lucknow, the number of girls per thousand has also increased in Mau, Mainpuri, Bijnor, Unnao and Balrampur
 abhi bhi kai jile bure haal main hai
 There are about 27 districts, including Rae Bareli, Faizabad, Ghaziabad, Chitrakoot, Hapur, where the number of girls per thousand has decreased
 uttar pradesh main 2016-17 main kul 36 lakh 62 hajaar se zyada bacchon ne janm liya tha
 Out of which 19 lakh were more than 21 thousand boys and more than 17 lakh 41 thousand girls, but so far this year more than 35 lakh children have been born
 jisamen 18 lakh 69 hajaar se adhik ladke hai or 17 lakh 3 hajaar se adhik ladkiyaan hai

 Learn about Motilal Nehru's life
 
 
 
 - Motilal Nehru was born on 6 May 1861
 unke pita kaa naam gangadhar nehru tha, jinka moti laal nehru ke janm se teen maheene pehle hi nidhan ho gaya

 baad main wo elahabaad chale gaye

 - 1919 se 1920 or 1928 se 1929 ke dauraan moti laal nehru do baar congress ke adhyaksh rahe

 jab china ke paas nahin tha koi vimaan, nehru ne bheja to dilli aae the PM- gulam bharat ke dauraan unhone nehru report likhi, jo kisi bhi bhartiya kaa pehla likhit samvidhan mana jaataa he

 lekin loksabhaa kii tarah rajyasabha main bhi congress ke haath kaa saath modi sarkaar ke saath ho, ye jaruri nahin

 iske jariye congress saansadon ne jis sanshodhan kii baat sadan main uthaai thi, jinamein sajaa ke praavdhaan ko kam karne or pati ke jail jane par jurmaane kii baat kahi gai he, use wo rajyasabha main bill main shaamil karne ke liye dabaav bana sakati he
 The opposition has a substantial number of forces and majority in the Rajya Sabha
 isiilie mana ja rahaa he ki congress sahit vipaksh dal ekajute hokar modi sarkaar par sanshodhan ke liye dabaav banane or use sansadeey samiti ke paas bhejne ke liye aagrah karke mushkilen khadi karenge
 Who has the strength in the Rajya Sabha? There are 28 political parties in the 245-member Rajya Sabha, except the independents and nominated members, whose members are there

 ardhsainik bal frontier corps ke pravaktaa vasay khan ne kaha ki maare gaye or 123 ghayalon main se zyaadaatar cadet or sainik the

 puure pakistan main hamale ke baad dehshat kaa maahaul he, or log rah-rahakar varsh 2014 main peshawar main sena ke skool par hue taliban aatankwaadiyon ke hamale ko yaad kar rahe hai, jisamen 150 log maare gaye the, jinamein zyaadaatar bachche the

 hamane ek team banaai he
 They are studying the details assuming the leaks
 ' parrikar ne kaha, 'doosraa pahalu qaraar sambandhi patibaddhta or uchit soochna kaa he jo hamane maangi he
 We are waiting for their reply
 jawaab aa jaae
 (apart from the headline, this news has not been edited by the NDTV team, it has been published directly from the Syndicate feed
 ) However, the Defense Minister also said that he is speaking based on the information given to him by the Navy
 unhone kaha ki chintaa ke kuch kshetra jarur hai kyonki mantralay sabase kharaab sthiti ko dhyaan main rakhkar aage bad rahaa he
 He also clarified that the leaking of documents related to the Scorpene submarines would not affect any deal being made with France, including the Rafale fighter aircraft deal
 raksha mantri ne kaha ki 'da australian' akhbaar ke web portal par daale gaye li dastavejon main scorpine kii kisi shastr pranali kaa ullekh nahin he jaisaa ki media main khabar ai
 Parrikar said that the Navy has assured him that most of the leaked documents are not going to cause concern
 unhone kaha, 'shastr pranali ke samjhaute shastr nirmaataaon ke saath hai or ve alag samjhaute hai
 Secondly, not all the submarines have been sea tested yet
 isliye sabase adhik mahatvapurn cheez (pandubbi kii gatividhi) dastavejon main shaamil nahin he
 But a few hours later, journalist Cameron Stewart said that these things were also leaked
 stewart ne hi mumbai main france kii company disienes ke saath saajhedaari main bhartiya nausena ke liye banaai ja rahi chah atyaadhunik pandubbiyon kii kshamtaaon se sambandhit atyant gopneey jaankaree ke 22,000 se adhik prishth li hone se sambandhit khabar prakashit kii thi
 Stewart tweeted, 'indian Defense Minister says leaked information on Scorpene submarines does not include weapon system information
 galat he
 We will release documents related to weapons on Monday
 ' unhone kaha, 'jab main kah rahaa hum ki ham scorpine shastr pranali par li hue dastavej jari karenge to usamen jaahir taur par samvedansheel soochnaaon kaa ham sampadan karenge
 ' raksha mantralay ke sutron ne bhi li ko tavajjo nahin dete hue kaha he ki yah rashtriya suraksha ke saath samjhauta nahin karata, kyonki dastavej puraane hai or isamen shastr pranali kaa byoraa nahin he
 The Defense Minister also said that the Scorpene Panudbubi has not completed sea trials which is important to understand how it will work underwater
 bhartiya nausena ne scorpine dastavej li maamle ko france ke shastreekaran mahanideshak ke saath uthaaya he
 Parrikar told reporters on the sidelines of a seminar organized by defense website Bharatshakti
in, 'we are waiting for the report
 vastav main website par daali gai saamagree badi chintaa vaali nahin he
 We are automatically assuming that it has been leaked and we are all taking precaution
 ' Parrikar said, "from what i have been told, there are some areas of concern to believe that the leak which has been claimed to have been leaked is indeed leaked
 ' unhone kaha, 'ham ise sabase buree sthiti maan rahe hai
 But i think that is not a big concern because we will be able to put things in the right perspective
 ' ek patrkaar ne jab poocha ki kya li hone se rafel saude par asar padegaa, to raksha mantri ne palat kar sawaal kiya ki kya koi france kii kisi company ke utpaadon kaa istemaal isliye band kar degaa, kyonki duusari company main jaankaree li ho gai
 Parrikar said that the action should be based on the conditions mentioned in the tender
 france se ai media kii khabaron ke anusaar dastavej disienes ke ek purv karmchaaree ne churaae, vahiin bharat ko is bare main kuch bhi likhit main nahin mila he
 More than 22,000 pages of highly confidential information related to the capabilities of the six state-of-the-art submarines released to the Indian Navy in partnership with a French company in Mumbai were leaked, leading to security concerns
 majgaanv godi main francisi pot nirmaataa company disienes dwaara 3
 Information related to the combat capability of the Scorpene submarines being built at a cost of $ 5 billion became public when the Australian newspaper put it on its website
 jab raksha mantri se poocha gaya ki kya disienes ko li ke bare main bharat ko suchit nahin karnaa chahie tha, jo 2011 main hone kii baat kahi ja rahi he to parrikar ne kaha ki sarkaar company se aadhikarik jawaab kaa intjaar karegi
 The comments unhone kaha, 'ek pahalu suraksha kaa he jo hamaare liye pehali praathamikta he
 We have formed a team
 ve li hone kii baat maanakar byore kaa adhyayan kar rahe hai
 Parrikar said, "the second aspect is the commitment to the agreement and the proper information that we have sought
 ham unke jawaab kaa intjaar kar rahe hai

 The Indian Navy has taken up the Scorpene Document Leak Case with the Director General of Arms of France
 parrikar ne raksha website bharatshakti dot in dwaara yojit ek seminar se itar samvaadadaataaon se kaha, 'hamen report kaa intjaar he
 Actually the content put on the website is not a big concern
 ham apane aap maan rahe hai ki yah li hui he or ham sabhi ehtiyaat barat rahe hai
 ' parrikar ne kaha, 'jo mujhe bataaya gaya he, uske anusaar yah maanate hue kuch chintaa ke kshetra hai ki jo li hone kaa daawa kiya gaya he, vah vaaki main li hua he
 'they said,' We are considering it the worst case scenario
 lekin mujhe lagata he ki badi chintaa vaali baat nahin he kyonki ham sahi pariprekshya main chizon ko rakhane main safal honge
 When a journalist asked if the leak would affect the Rafale deal, the defense minister retorted and asked if anyone would stop using products from a French company because information was leaked at another company
 parrikar ne kaha ki karrwai nivida main ullikhit sharton par aadhaarit honi chahie
 According to media reports from France, the documents were stolen by a former DCNS employee, while India has not found anything in writing about it
